TITLE       New total neutron cross section measurement of uranium20016  1    3 
            between 0.5 to 4.35 MeV                               20016  1    4 
INSTITUTE  (2GERKFK)                                              20016  1    5 
REFERENCE  ((C,70HELSINKI,2,39,1970)=(R,KFK-1199,1970))           20016  1    6 
           (W,NEBE,197012)        cross section on tape.          20016  1    7 
REL-REF    (I,,S.Cierjacks+,J,RSI,39,1279,1968)                   20016  1    8 
AUTHOR     (D.Kopsch, S.Cierjacks, G.J.Kirouac)                   20016  1    9 
FACILITY   (ISOCY,2GERKFK) 45 MeV karlsruhe isochronous cyclotron 20016  1   10 
           .Deuteron burst width 1 ns, repetition rate 20 kc/s.   20016  1   11 
INC-SOURCE            U(d,nx)-reaction.                           20016  1   12 
INC-SPECT   Broad neutron spectrum in the energy region from      20016  1   13 
            0.3 to 30 MeV.                                        20016  1   14 
SAMPLE      Natural uranium with thickness 0.09542 atoms/barn.    20016  1   15 
            Sample impurities were ascertained to contribute      20016  1   16 
            less than 0.3%.                                       20016  1   17 
METHOD     (TOF)  Time of flight path = 187.5 m.                  20016  1   18 
           .Overall time resolution = 5.48 nsec. (See comment)    20016  1   19 
                      transmission measurement.                   20016  1   20 
           .The neutron beam was collimated at 1 m, 10 m and 37 m 20016  1   21 
            from the source to about 2.E-6 sr.                    20016  1   22 
           .The sample was positioned at 1.5 m from the source.   20016  1   23 
           .Alternating runs with the sample in and out of the    20016  1   24 
            beam on a 250 sec cycle.                              20016  1   25 
DETECTOR   (SCIN)  proton recoil plastic scintillator,            20016  1   26 
            NE102A, 25 cm diameter 1 cm thick,                    20016  1   27 
            viewed simultaneously by two XP-1040 phototubes.      20016  1   28 
COMMENT    .The resolution of 0.029 ns/m corresponds to an energy 20016  1   29 
            resolution of about 290 eV at 0.5 MeV and 7.44 keV at 20016  1   30 
            4.35 MeV. The purpose of this work was to perform a   20016  1   31 
            high resolution total cross section measurement with  20016  1   32 
            good statistics.                                      20016  1   33 
           .More than 3000 data points were obtained and the      20016  1   34 
            results are in good agreement with other data except  20016  1   35 
            some older measurements.                              20016  1   36 
CORRECTION  In the sample  out  position, the average counting    20016  1   37 
            rate for the detector was about 0.4 neutrons per      20016  1   38 
            machine burst.                                        20016  1   39 
            Up to 3 counts per machine burst could be accepted by 20016  1   40 
            the time analyzer and data acquisition system.        20016  1   41 
            Corrected for background and                          20016  1   42 
            for the dead time of the time recording system.       20016  1   43 
            Multiple scattering effects are estimated to be       20016  1   44 
            negligible.                                           20016  1   45 
ERR-ANALYS  The resolution width in the final reduced data        20016  1   46 
            corresponds to 1.37 times the point spacing.          20016  1   47 
           (ERR-S,0.45,2.58) The statistical uncertainty lies     20016  1   48 
            between 0.45% at 4.35 MeV and 2.58% at 0.5 MeV.       20016  1   49 
           (ERR-1,,3.) The effects of sample impurities were      20016  1   50 
            ascertained to contribute less than 3% uncertainty to 20016  1   51 
            the cross-section.                                    20016  1   52 
           (DATA-ERR) No information about source of uncertainties20016  1   53
